          <script>
           // some common functions
    function sbInp_clearPlaceholder(sbox) {
        sbox = $(sbox);
        if (sbox.hasClass('searchBoxEmpty')) {
            sbox.removeClass('searchBoxEmpty').val('').removeAttr('placeholder');
        }
    }
    function sbInp_syncPlaceholder(sbox) {
        sbox = $(sbox);
        sbox.removeClass('searchBoxEmpty');
        var emptyText = sbox.attr('data-empty');
        if ($.trim(sbox.val()).length == 0 || $.trim(sbox.val()) == emptyText) {
            sbox.addClass('searchBoxEmpty').val(emptyText).attr('placeholder', emptyText);
        }
    }
          </script>

    var _hideForCertainPages = false;
    $('#dnn_dnnBreadcrumb_lblBreadCrumb').children('span').each(function () {
        $(this).children('span').each(function (a, b) {
            var _breadCrumbText = $(b).text().toLowerCase();
            //if (_breadCrumbText.indexOf("research areas") > -1 || _breadCrumbText.indexOf("membership") > -1) {
            //    _hideForCertainPages = true;
            //}

                $(b).hide();
            }
            if (_breadCrumbText.indexOf("conference microsites") > -1 || _breadCrumbText.indexOf("an17") > -1) {
                _hideForCertainPages = true;
            }


        })
    });

        $('.breadcrumbs-container').show();

    else {
        $('.breadcrumbs-container').hide();
    }

       // shim layer with setTimeout fallback
  window.requestAnimFrame = (function(){
    return  window.requestAnimationFrame       ||
            window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame ||
            window.mozRequestAnimationFrame    ||
            window.oRequestAnimationFrame      ||
            window.msRequestAnimationFrame     ||
            function( callback ){
              window.setTimeout(callback, 1000 / 60);
            };
  })();

  (function(win, d) {

    var DQSB = d.querySelector.bind(d);

    var shape1 = DQSB('#shape-1_1770');
    var shape2 = DQSB('#shape-2_1770');
    var shape3 = DQSB('#shape-3_1770');

    //var pos = jQuery("#confetti").position().top;
    //console.log(pos);

    var ticking = false;
        var lastScrollY = 0;

        function onResize() {
            updateElements(win.pageYOffset);
        }

        function onScroll(evt) {

            if (!ticking) {
                ticking = true;
                requestAnimFrame(updateElements);
                lastScrollY = win.pageYOffset;
            }
        }

        function updateElements() {
            var posit = jQuery("#confetti_1770").offset().top;

            var relativeY = lastScrollY / (posit + 2000);

            mainBG.style.backgroundPosition = 'center' + pos(0, 0, relativeY, 0) + 'px';

            shape1.style.top = pos(100, -1300, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape1.style.left = 15 + '%';

            shape2.style.top = pos(-824, -5400, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape2.style.left = 1 + '%';

            shape3.style.top = pos(-200, -2600, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape3.style.right = 12 + '%';

            shape4.style.top = pos(-800, -2000, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape4.style.left = 60 + '%';

            shape5.style.top = pos(-1080, -1800, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape5.style.left = 12 + '%';

            shape6.style.top = pos(60, -9700, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape6.style.left = 55 + '%';

            shape7.style.top = pos(350, -2400, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape7.style.left = 75 + '%';

            shape8.style.top = pos(300, -2700, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape8.style.left = 90 + '%';

            shape9.style.top = pos(-800, -1200, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape9.style.left = 28 + '%';

            shape10.style.top = pos(-200, -900, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape10.style.left = 95 + '%';

            shape11.style.top = pos(42, -920, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape11.style.left = 36 + '%';

            shape12.style.top = pos(392, -1220, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape12.style.left = 29 + '%';

            shape13.style.top = pos(-900, -1400, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape13.style.left = 14 + '%';

            shape14.style.top = pos(640, -1420, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape14.style.left = 74 + '%';

            shape15.style.top = pos(920, -1520, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape15.style.left = 4 + '%';

            shape16.style.top = pos(720, -1520, relativeY, 0) + 'px';
            shape16.style.left = 44 + '%';

            ticking = false;
        }

    function pos(base, range, relY, offset) {
      return base + limit(0, 1, relY - offset) * range;
    }

    function prefix(obj, prop, value) {
      var prefs = ['webkit', 'moz', 'o', 'ms'];
      for (var pref in prefs) {
        obj[prefs[pref] + prop] = value;
      }
    }

    function limit(min, max, value) {
      return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
    }

    (function() {

      updateElements(win.pageYOffset);

      shape1.classList.add('force-show');
      shape2.classList.add('force-show');
      shape3.classList.add('force-show');
      shape4.classList.add('force-show');
      shape5.classList.add('force-show');
      shape6.classList.add('force-show');
      shape7.classList.add('force-show');
      shape8.classList.add('force-show');
      shape9.classList.add('force-show');
    })();

    win.addEventListener('resize', onResize, false);
    win.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, false);

  })(window, document);
      </script>
     </div>

           <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function() {             
            var input = document.getElementById("search-text");             
            var _newURl = "";             
            $('#journal-checkboxlist').click(function() {                 
                var checkboxes = document.getElementById("jn_list");                 
                if (checkboxes.style.display == "none") {                     
                    checkboxes.style.display = "block";                 
                } 
                else {                     
                    checkboxes.style.display = "none";                 
                }             
            });             
            $(document).click(function(evt) {                 
                var target = evt.target.className;                 
                if ($.trim(target) != '') {                     
                    if ("." + target != ".overSelect" && target != "jb-inpselect hs-journal-search-height" && target != 'selectBox' && target != 'multiselect homescreen-journal-search-width hs-multiselect-dd' && target != 'embed-submit-field hs-journal-custom' && target != 'journal-search-container homescreen-search') {                         
                        document.getElementById("jn_list").style.display = "none";                     
                    }                 
                }             
            });              
            function DetectMobile(url) {             
                if (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/webOS/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i) || navigator.userAgent.match(/Windows Phone/i)) {                  
                    return "http://epubs.siam.org/#/action/doMobileSearch?startPage=0&searchText=";                 
                } 
                else {                  
                    return "http://epubs.siam.org/action/doSearch?AllField=";                 
                }             
            }              
            function navigateWithParams(uri) {                 
                var _count = 0;  
                console.log(uri);               
                $('#jn_list input:checked').each(function() {                     
                    _count++;                 
                });                 
                if (_count == 0) {                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + input.value;                 
                } 
                else {                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + input.value;                     
                    $('#jn_list input:checked').each(function() {                         
                        _newURl  = _newURl + "&publication=" +  $(this).attr('id');                     
                    });                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + "&AfterMonth=&AfterYear=&BeforeMonth=&BeforeYear=";                 
                }                 
                if ($("#volume_val").val()) {                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + "&volume=" + $("#volume_val").val()                 
                }                 
                if ($("#issue_val").val()) {                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + "&issue=" + $("#issue_val").val()                 
                }                 
                if ($("#page_val").val()) {                     
                    _newURl  = _newURl + "&startPage=" + $("#page_val").val()                 
                }                 
                window.open(_newURl, '_blank').focus();                 
                _newURl = "";                 
                return false;             
            }             
            $("#search-journal").click(function() {                 
                _newURl = DetectMobile();                 
                navigateWithParams(_newURl);             
            });             
            $(".jn-input_search").keyup(function(e) {                 
                if ((e.keyCode === 13)) {                     
                    _newURl = DetectMobile();                     
                    navigateWithParams(_newURl);                 
                }             
            });             
            $('.jn-mobileonly-x-icon').click(function () {                 
                input.value = "";                 
                $('.jn-mobileonly-x-icon').css("display", "none");             
            });              
            $(".jn-searcharea").keyup(function (e) {                 
                if ((e.keyCode === 13)) {                     
                    _newURl = DetectMobile();                     
                    navigateWithParams(_newURl);                 
                } 
                else {                     
                    if (input.value.length > 0) {                         
                        $('.jn-mobileonly-x-icon').css("display", "block");                     
                    } 
                    else {                         
                        $('.jn-mobileonly-x-icon').css("display", "none");                     
                    }                 
            }             
         });         
     });
           </script>

            $(document).ready(function () {        var newsTitles = [];        var _initLoadOut = 3;        function RenderNewsFeed() {            var _rssLink = "https://sinews.siam.org/Article-Feed/rss/2819";                        var _rtn;            /* This is to limit initial count of items.*/            var encodedURL = encodeURIComponent(_rssLink);                        $.ajax({                type: 'GET',                contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=UTF-8",                url: location.protocol + '//' + location.hostname + '/WS%20RSS/RSSFeed.asmx/GetWhatsNewRSS',                data: { url: encodedURL },                success: function (data) {                    var str = data.childNodes[0].firstChild.nodeValue.toString();                    _rtn = JSON.parse(str);                                        FilterItemsForDisplay(_rtn.rss.channel);                    $(function(){var siNewsHomeSwiper= new BrioSwiper(".homepage-sinews-home-grid-swiper", ".homepage-sinews-home-grid-swiper-pagination");});                },                error: function (e) {                }                });        }        function FilterItemsForDisplay(obj) {            var browserWidth = $(window).width();                        obj.item = obj.item.sort(function (a, b) {                return new Date(b.pubDate).getTime() - new Date(a.pubDate).getTime()            });            var _appendHTML = "<div class='siam-news-grid-white-bg'><a href='https://sinews.siam.org' target='blank' style='border-bottom:none !important'><img class='sinews-logo' src='https://s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/s.cdpn.io/858178/sinews-logo.jpg'></a></div>";            var _mobileHTML = "";            var _count = 0;            if (obj.item.length < _initLoadOut) {                _count = obj.item.length;            }            else {                _count = _initLoadOut;            }            for (var i = 0; i < _count; i++) {                var _pubDate = "";                var _link = "";                var _title = "";                var _paneColor = "";                switch(i) {                    case 0:                        _paneColor = "siam-news-grid-teal-bg";                    break;                    case 1:                        _paneColor = "siam-news-grid-pink-bg";                    break;                    case 2:                        _paneColor = "siam-news-grid-orange-bg";                    break;                }                                _title = obj.item[i].title['#cdata-section'];                _link = obj.item[i].link;                _pubDate = obj.item[i].pubDate;                var dt = new Date(_pubDate);                dt = dt.format('MMMM d, yyyy');                newsTitles.push(_title);                if(browserWidth >= 1225 && browserWidth < 1620){                    if (_title.length > 85){                    var cutoffTitle = _title.substring(0, 86);                        _appendHTML += "<div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + " clickableDiv'><h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                     "<div class='home-grid-news-content tooltip'>" + cutoffTitle + " . . .<span class='tooltiptext'>" + _title + "</span></div>" +                     "<span class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow'>Read More</span></div>";                    }                    else {                        _appendHTML += "<div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + " clickableDiv'><h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                     "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title + "</div>" +                     "<span class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow'>Read More</span></div>";                    }                                   }                else if(browserWidth < 1225 && browserWidth > 1008){                    if (_title.length > 60){                    var cutoffTitle = _title.substring(0, 61);                        _appendHTML += "<div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + " clickableDiv'><h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                     "<div class='home-grid-news-content tooltip'>" + cutoffTitle + " . . .<span class='tooltiptext'>" + _title + "</span></div>" +                     "<span class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow'>Read More</span></div>";                    }                    else {                        _appendHTML += "<div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + " clickableDiv'><h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                     "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title + "</div>" +                     "<span class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow'>Read More</span></div>";                    }                   }                else {                    _appendHTML += "<div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + " clickableDiv'><h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                     "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title + "</div>" +                     "<span class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow'>Read More</span></div>";                }                if (i == 0){                    _mobileHTML += "<div class='swiper-slide swiper-slide-active'><div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + "'>" +                    "<h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                    "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title +                     "</div><a class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow' href='" + _link + "' target='_blank'>Read More</a></div></div>";                }                else if(i == 1){                    _mobileHTML += "<div class='swiper-slide swiper-slide-next'><div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + "'>" +                "<h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title +                 "</div><a class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow' href='" + _link + "' target='_blank'>Read More</a></div></div>";                }                else {                    _mobileHTML += "<div class='swiper-slide'><div onclick=\"window.open('" +  _link + "')\"class='" + _paneColor + "'>" +                "<h6 class='display-font'>" + dt.toString() + "</h6>" +                "<div class='home-grid-news-content'>" + _title +                 "</div><a class='button-dark-mobile-white-arrow' href='" + _link + "' target='_blank'>Read More</a></div></div>";                }                            }            $('.siam-news-grid-home-container').html(_appendHTML);            $('.homepage-siam-news-mobile').html(_mobileHTML);        }        RenderNewsFeed();        $(window).resize(function() {              var browserWidth = $(window).width();                 if(browserWidth >= 1225 && browserWidth < 1620){                HandleLongTitleOnScreenResize(newsTitles, 85);            }            else if(browserWidth < 1225 && browserWidth > 1008){                HandleLongTitleOnScreenResize(newsTitles, 60);            }            else{                var newsTeal = $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-teal-bg .home-grid-news-content");                if (typeof newsTeal[0] !== 'undefined' && newsTeal[0].className == "home-grid-news-content tooltip"){                    newsTeal.removeClass("tooltip");                    newsTeal.html(newsTitles[0]);                }                var newsPink = $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-pink-bg .home-grid-news-content");                if (typeof newsPink[0] !== 'undefined' && newsPink[0].className == "home-grid-news-content tooltip"){                    newsPink.addClass("tooltip");                    newsPink.html(newsTitles[0]);                }                var newsOrange = $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-orange-bg .home-grid-news-content");                if (typeof newsOrange[0] !== 'undefined' && newsOrange[0].className == "home-grid-news-content tooltip"){                    newsOrange.addClass("tooltip");                    newsOrange.html(newsTitles[0]);                }            }        });                function HandleLongTitleOnScreenResize(newsTitles, charLimit){            for(var i = 0; i < newsTitles.length; i++){                if (newsTitles[i].length > charLimit){                    var cutoffTitle = newsTitles[i].substring(0, charLimit + 1) + " . . .";                         if(i == 0){                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-teal-bg .home-grid-news-content").html(cutoffTitle);                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-teal-bg .home-grid-news-content").addClass("tooltip");                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-teal-bg .home-grid-news-content").append("<span class='tooltiptext'>" + newsTitles[i] + "</span>");                    }                    else if(i == 1){                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-pink-bg .home-grid-news-content").html(cutoffTitle);                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-pink-bg .home-grid-news-content").addClass("tooltip");                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-pink-bg .home-grid-news-content").append("<span class='tooltiptext'>" + newsTitles[i] + "</span>");                    }                       else if(i == 2){                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-orange-bg .home-grid-news-content").html(cutoffTitle);                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-orange-bg .home-grid-news-content").addClass("tooltip");                        $(".siam-news-grid-home-container.desktop-only .siam-news-grid-orange-bg .home-grid-news-content").append("<span class='tooltiptext'>" + newsTitles[i] + "</span>");                    }                                                   }            }        }            });

                    "color": "#283d6a"

        heatmap = new google.maps.visualization.HeatmapLayer({
            data: getPoints(),
            map: map,
            radius: 40
        });

        toggleHeatmap();

        setMarkers(map, sections, markerTypes[0]);
        setMarkers(map, chapters, markerTypes[1]);
        setMarkers(map, conferenceGroups, markerTypes[2]);
        setMarkers(map, membershipMarkerArr, markerTypes[3]);

        globalMapCenter = map.getCenter();
        ////////////////////////
        // SEARCH BOX ///
        var input = document.getElementById('pac-input');
        var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(
          input, {
            fields: ['place_id']
          });
        autocomplete.bindTo('bounds', map);

        map.controls[google.maps.ControlPosition.TOP_LEFT].push(input);

        var infowindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow();
        var infowindowContent = document.getElementById('infowindow-content');
        infowindow.setContent(infowindowContent);
        var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder;
        var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
            map: map
        });
        marker.addListener('click', function () {
            infowindow.open(map, marker);
        });

        autocomplete.addListener('place_changed', function () {
            infowindow.close();
            var place = autocomplete.getPlace();

            if (!place.place_id) {
                return;
            }
            geocoder.geocode({
                'placeId': place.place_id
            }, function (results, status) {

                if (status !== 'OK') {
                    window.alert('Geocoder failed due to: ' + status);
                    return;
                }
                map.setZoom(11);
                map.setCenter(results[0].geometry.location);
                // Set the position of the marker using the place ID and location.
                marker.setPlace({
                    placeId: place.place_id,
                    location: results[0].geometry.location
                });
                marker.setVisible(true);
                infowindowContent.children['place-name'].textContent = place.name;
                infowindowContent.children['place-id'].textContent = place.place_id;
                infowindowContent.children['place-address'].textContent =
                  results[0].formatted_address;
                infowindow.open(map, marker);
            });
        });
        ////////////////////////

    } //End of function initMap

    ////////////////////////

    var allChapterMarkers = [];
    var allSectionMarkers = [];
    var allConferenceMarkers = [];
    var allMembershipMarkers = [];

    var mouseOnMarker = false;
    var clickedToKeepTooltipOpen = false;
    var timer = null;

    var middleMarker;
    var outsideMarker;

    var showTooltipFunctions = {}

    function setMarkers(map, markers, markerType) {
        var insideCircle = getInsideCircle(markerType);
        var middleCircle = getMiddleCircle(markerType);
        var outsideCircle;


        // RESIZE THE OUTSIDE CIRCLE OF THE "SECTION" MARKER WHEN ZOOMING THE MAP
        google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'zoom_changed', googleMapsZoomChanged);

        for (var i = 0; i < markers.length; i++) {

            var latToUse = markerType.Type === "conference"
                ? markers[i][0].Lat
                : markers[i].Lat;
            
            var lngToUse = markerType.Type === "conference"
                ? markers[i][0].Lng
                : markers[i].Lng;

            var markerIdToUse = markerType.Type === "conference"
                ? markers[i][0].MarkerId
                : markers[i].MarkerId;

            var insideMarker = new google.maps.Marker({
                position: {
                    lat: latToUse,
                    lng: lngToUse
                },
                icon: insideCircle,
                map: map,
                optimized: false,
                zIndex: 1010,
                MarkerId: markerIdToUse
            });

            insideMarker.setVisible(false);

            if (markerType.Type == "section") {
                allSectionMarkers.push(insideMarker);
            } else if (markerType.Type == "chapter") {
                allChapterMarkers.push(insideMarker);
            } else if( markerType.Type == "conference"){
                allConferenceMarkers.push(insideMarker);
            } else if( markerType.Type == "membership"){
                allMembershipMarkers.push(insideMarker);
            }

            if("Membership" == "Section" && markerType.Type == "section"){
                insideMarker.setVisible(true);
                $('.mapBtn.sectionBtn').addClass("sectionOnSelected");
            }
            else if("Membership" == "Student Chapter" && markerType.Type == "chapter"){
                insideMarker.setVisible(true);
                $('.mapBtn.chapterBtn').addClass("chapterOnSelected");
            }
            else if("Membership" == "Conference" && markerType.Type == "conference"){
                insideMarker.setVisible(true);
                $('.mapBtn.conferenceBtn').addClass("conferenceOnSelected");
            }
            else if("Membership" == "Membership" && markerType.Type == "membership"){
                insideMarker.setVisible(true);
                $('.mapBtn.membershipBtn').addClass("membershipOnSelected");
            }

            var locationToUse =  markerType.Type === "conference"
                ? markers[i][0].Location
                : markers[i].Location;

            insideMarker.outsideRadius = markers[i].Radius;
            insideMarker.title = markers[i].Name;
            insideMarker.location = locationToUse;
            insideMarker.member = markers[i].Member;

            insideMarker.tooltipContent = "";

            if (markerType.Type == "conference") {

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<table class='desktop-only'><tr>";

                for(var j = 0; j < markers[i].length; j++)
                {
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<td class='bold marker-tooltip-content'>" + markers[i][j].Name + "</td>";
                }

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</tr><tr>";

                for(var j = 0; j < markers[i].length; j++)
                {
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<td class='marker-tooltip-content'>" + markers[i][j].Location + "</td>";
                }

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</tr><tr>";

                for(var j = 0; j < markers[i].length; j++)
                {
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<td class='italic marker-tooltip-content'>" + markers[i][j].Member + "</td>";
                }

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</tr><tr>";

                for(var j = 0; j < markers[i].length; j++)
                {
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<td class='marker-tooltip-content'><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i][j].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a></td>";
                }

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</tr></table>";

                // mobile view
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='mobile-only swiper-container map-swiper-container'><div class='swiper-wrapper map-swiper-wrapper'>";

                for(var j = 0; j < markers[i].length; j++)
                {
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='swiper-slide map-swiper-slide'>";
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div class='bold'>" + markers[i][j].Name + "</div><br/>";
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + markers[i][j].Location + "</div><br/>";
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div class='italic'>" + markers[i][j].Member + "</div><br/>";
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i][j].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a></div><br/>"
                    insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div>";
                }

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div><div class='swiper-button-prev map-swiper-button-prev'></div><div class='swiper-button-next map-swiper-button-next'></div></div>";
                // end mobile view
            }

            else if (isNaN(insideMarker.member) && markerType.Type != "membership") {

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='marker-tooltip-content'>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.title + "<br/></div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.location + "<br/></div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.member + "<br/></div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a><br/><br/></div>"
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div>";
            }
            else if (markerType.Type == "section") {
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='marker-tooltip-content'>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.title + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.location + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.member + " Members</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a><br/><br/></div>"
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div>";

            }
            else if (markerType.Type == "membership") {
                var plural = insideMarker.title <= 1
                    ? ""
                    : "S";

                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='marker-tooltip-content'>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.title + " MEMBER" + plural + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.location + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a><br/><br/></div>"
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div>";

            }
            else {
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "<div class='marker-tooltip-content'>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.title + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.location + "</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div>" + insideMarker.member + " Student Members</div>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <hr/>";
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "    <div><a class='tooltip-link' target='_blank' href='" + markers[i].Website + "'>LEARN MORE</a><br/><br/></div>"
                insideMarker.tooltipContent += "</div>";
            }

            insideMarker.addListener('mouseover', function (e) {
                onMouseOver(this, e);
            });

            insideMarker.addListener('mouseout', insideMarkerMouseOut);

            var f = getInsideMarkerClickedFunction(insideMarker)
            google.maps.event.addListener(insideMarker, 'click', f);

        } // end of for loop

        // The function creation is inside another function
        // so that the reference to this specific "insideMarker" can be preserved
        function getInsideMarkerClickedFunction(marker) {
            return function (ev) {
                insideMarkerClicked(marker, ev)
            }
        }

        function onMouseOver(this1, e, shouldHideTooltip = false) {
            if (shouldHideTooltip) {
                hideTooltip();
            }

            e = e || window.event;

            var eventToUse = (!e.clientX || !e.clientY)
                ? e[Object.keys(e)[1]]
                : e;

            mouseOver(eventToUse, this1.position.lat(), this1.position.lng(), this1.getPosition(), map, this1.tooltipContent, this1.outsideRadius, markerType);

            myMarker = this1;
            mouseOnMarker = true;
        }

        function showTooltip(event, lat, lng, position, map, content, outsideRadius, markerType) {
            if (outsideMarker != null) { outsideMarker.setMap(null); }
            if (middleMarker != null) { middleMarker.setMap(null); }
            middleMarker = new google.maps.Marker({
                position: {
                    lat: lat,
                    lng: lng
                },
                icon: middleCircle,
                map: map,
                optimized: false,
                zIndex: 1002
            });
            outsideMarker = new google.maps.Marker({
                position: {
                    lat: lat,
                    lng: lng
                },
                icon: outsideCircle,
                map: map,
                optimized: false,
                zIndex: 1001
            });


            $('#marker-tooltip').html('<div id="marker-tooltip-overlay">' + content + '</div>').show();

            var tooltipCoords = getTooltipCoords(event);

            $('#marker-tooltip').css({
                'left': tooltipCoords.xPoint + 'px',
                'top': tooltipCoords.yPoint + 'px',
                'background-color': markerType.PanelColor
            });

            $('hr').css({ 'background-color': markerType.PanelColor, 'color': markerType.PanelColor });

            if (markerType.Type === 'conference') {
                mapSwiper = new Swiper ('.map-swiper-container', {
                    slideClass: 'map-swiper-slide',
                    wrapperClass: 'map-swiper-wrapper',
                    navigation: {
                      nextEl: '.map-swiper-button-next',
                      prevEl: '.map-swiper-button-prev',
                      disabledClass: 'map-swiper-button-disabled'
                    }
              })
            }
        }

        function mouseOver(event, lat, lng, position, map, content, outsideRadius, markerType) {
            if (clickedToKeepTooltipOpen) {
                return;
            }

            outsideCircle = getOutsideCircle(outsideRadius, map, markerType);
            clearTimeout(timer);
            clickedToKeepTooltipOpen = false;
            timer = setTimeout(function () {
                showTooltip(event, lat, lng, position, map, content, outsideRadius, markerType);
            }, 120);

        } //end of mouseOver


        function insideMarkerMouseOut() {
            if (!clickedToKeepTooltipOpen) {
                hideTooltip();
            }
        }

        function insideMarkerClicked(marker, e) {
            if (clickedToKeepTooltipOpen) {
                onMouseOver(marker, e, true);
            }
            clickedToKeepTooltipOpen = true;
        }

        // Remove tooltip when scrolling off map
        window.addEventListener('scroll', throttle(checkRemoveTooltip, 300));

        function throttle(fn, wait) {
          var time = Date.now();
          return function() {
            if ((time + wait - Date.now()) < 0) {
              fn();
              time = Date.now();
            }
          }
        }

        function checkRemoveTooltip() {        
            var tooltipBounds = document.getElementById('marker-tooltip').getBoundingClientRect()

            if (tooltipBounds.height === 0) {
                // tooltip is not showing
                return;
            }

            if (tooltipBounds.y < -10
                || tooltipBounds.y > window.innerHeight) {
                hideTooltip()
            }
        }


    } // end of setMarkers function


    function mapContainerClicked(event) {
        // "img" here is a map pin
        if ($(event.target).is('#marker-tooltip-overlay, img')
            || $(event.target).parents('#marker-tooltip').length > 0) {
            return
        }

        hideTooltip();
    }

    function hideTooltip() {
        mouseOnMarker = false;
        clickedToKeepTooltipOpen = false;
        clearTimeout(timer);
        if(outsideMarker != null){outsideMarker.setMap(null);}
        if(middleMarker != null){middleMarker.setMap(null);}
        $('#marker-tooltip').hide();
    }

    $('#map-container').on('click', mapContainerClicked);

    function getInsideCircle(markerType) {

        var insideCircle = {
            path: google.maps.SymbolPath.CIRCLE,
            scale: getMarkerSize(),
            strokeColor: markerType.MarkerColor
        };

        if(markerType.Type != "membership"){
            insideCircle.fillColor = markerType.MarkerColor;
            insideCircle.fillOpacity = 1;
        }
        else {
            insideCircle.fillColor = markerType.MarkerColor;
            insideCircle.strokeWeight = 1;
        }
        return insideCircle;
    }

    function getMiddleCircle(markerType) {
        return {
            path: google.maps.SymbolPath.CIRCLE,
            scale: getMiddleCircleScale(),
            strokeColor: markerType.MarkerColor,
            strokeWeight: 4
        };
    }

    function getOutsideCircle(outsideRadius, map, markerType) {

        var currentRadius;
        if (outsideRadius) {
            currentRadius = outsideRadius;
        } else {
            currentRadius = 0;
        }

        if(markerType == "section"){
            var zoom = map.getZoom();
            var metersPerPx = 156543.03392 * Math.cos(globalMapCenter.lat() * Math.PI / 180) / Math.pow(2, zoom);
            currentRadius = outsideRadius / metersPerPx;
        }

        return {
            path: google.maps.SymbolPath.CIRCLE,
            strokeColor: markerType.MarkerColor,
            strokeOpacity: 0.2,
            scale: currentRadius,
            fillColor: markerType.MarkerColor,
            fillOpacity: 0.005
        };
    }


    function googleMapsZoomChanged(event) {
        if (allSectionMarkers[0].getVisible() === false) {
            return;
        }

        event = event || window.event;
        clearTimeout(timer);
        if(outsideMarker){ outsideMarker.setMap(null); }
        if(middleMarker){ middleMarker.setMap(null); }
        if (mouseOnMarker) {

            var eventToUse = (!e.clientX || !e.clientY)
                ? e[Object.keys(e)[1]]
                : event;

            mouseOver(eventToUse, myMarker.position.lat(), myMarker.position.lng(), myMarker.getPosition(), map, myMarker.tooltipContent, myMarker.outsideRadius, "section");
        }
    }

    function getTooltipCoords(event) {
        var leftLoginBarWidth = $('#google-map').offset().left;
        var xPoint = 0;
        var yPoint = 0;

        var xOffset = leftLoginBarWidth > 0
            ? 50
            : leftLoginBarWidth + 30;

        if(event.type == "touchend")
        {
            xPoint = event.changedTouches[0].clientX + xOffset;
            yPoint = event.changedTouches[0].clientY;

        }
        else
        {
            xPoint = event.clientX + xOffset;
            yPoint = event.clientY;
        }

        var mapHeight = $("#google-map").height();
        var tooltipHeight = $("#marker-tooltip").height();

        var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop(),
        topEdgeToMapDiv = $('#google-map').offset().top,
        relativeTopEdgeToMapDiv = (topEdgeToMapDiv - scrollTop);

        if (yPoint > ($(window).height() - tooltipHeight - 20)) {
            yPoint = ($(window).height() - tooltipHeight -20);
        }
        else if (yPoint > (relativeTopEdgeToMapDiv + mapHeight - tooltipHeight)) {
            yPoint = (relativeTopEdgeToMapDiv + mapHeight - tooltipHeight);
        }

        if (yPoint < relativeTopEdgeToMapDiv + 20) {
            yPoint = relativeTopEdgeToMapDiv + 40;
        }

        if (xPoint > ($(window).width() - 400)) {
            xPoint -= 300;
            yPoint += 20;
        }

        return {
            xPoint: xPoint,
            yPoint: yPoint
        }
    }


    var membershipDefault = false;
    function toggleHeatmap() {
        var gradient = ['rgba(95,130,158, 0)',
                        'rgba(95,130,158, 1)',
                        '#5f829e',
                        '#587891',
                        '#516f87',
                        '#48647a',
                        '#394e61'];
        loadHeatmap = true;

        if (loadHeatmap == true) {
            if("Membership" != "Membership"){
                heatmap.setMap(heatmap.getMap() ? null : map);
            }

            heatmap.set('gradient', gradient);
            heatmap.set('radius', 40);
            heatmap.set('opacity', 1);
        }
    }

    // Membership
    $("#toggleHeatmapBtn").click(function(event){
        event.preventDefault();

        if (loadHeatmap == true) {
            if (heatmap.getMap()) {
                heatmap.setMap(null);
                $('.mapBtn.membershipBtn').removeClass("membershipOnSelected");
            } else {
                heatmap.setMap(map);
                $('.mapBtn.membershipBtn').addClass("membershipOnSelected");
            }

            for (var i = 0; i < allMembershipMarkers.length; i++) {
                var visibility;
                if(allMembershipMarkers[i].getVisible() == true){
                    visibility = false;
                }
                else {
                    visibility = true;
                }
                allMembershipMarkers[i].setVisible(visibility);
            }
        }
    });

    // Sections
    $("#yellowMarkers").click(function(event){
        event.preventDefault();
        for (var i = 0; i < allSectionMarkers.length; i++) {
            var visibility;
            if(allSectionMarkers[i].getVisible() == true){
                visibility = false;
                $('.mapBtn.sectionBtn').removeClass("sectionOnSelected");
            }
            else {
                visibility = true;
                $('.mapBtn.sectionBtn').addClass("sectionOnSelected");
            }
            allSectionMarkers[i].setVisible(visibility);
        }
    });

    // Student Chapters
    $("#blueMarkers").click(function(event){
        event.preventDefault();
        for (var i = 0; i < allChapterMarkers.length; i++) {
            var visibility;
            if(allChapterMarkers[i].getVisible() == true){
                visibility = false;
                $('.mapBtn.chapterBtn').removeClass("chapterOnSelected");
            }
            else {
                visibility = true;
                $('.mapBtn.chapterBtn').addClass("chapterOnSelected");
            }
            allChapterMarkers[i].setVisible(visibility);
        }
    });

    // Conferences
    $("#greenMarkers").click(function(event){
        event.preventDefault();
        for (var i = 0; i < allConferenceMarkers.length; i++) {
            var visibility;
            if(allConferenceMarkers[i].getVisible() == true){
                visibility = false;
                $('.mapBtn.conferenceBtn').removeClass("conferenceOnSelected");
            }
            else {
                visibility = true;
                $('.mapBtn.conferenceBtn').addClass("conferenceOnSelected");
            }
            allConferenceMarkers[i].setVisible(visibility);
        }
    });

    ////////////////////////
    ////////////////////////
    function fromLatLngToPoint(latLng, map) {
        var topRight = map.getProjection().fromLatLngToPoint(map.getBounds().getNorthEast());
        var bottomLeft = map.getProjection().fromLatLngToPoint(map.getBounds().getSouthWest());
        var scale = Math.pow(2, map.getZoom());
        var worldPoint = map.getProjection().fromLatLngToPoint(latLng);
        return new google.maps.Point((worldPoint.x - bottomLeft.x) * scale, (worldPoint.y - topRight.y) * scale);
    }

     <script>
      // some common functions
    function sbInp_clearPlaceholder(sbox) {
        sbox = $(sbox);
        if (sbox.hasClass('searchBoxEmpty')) {
            sbox.removeClass('searchBoxEmpty').val('').removeAttr('placeholder');
        }
    }
    function sbInp_syncPlaceholder(sbox) {
        sbox = $(sbox);
        sbox.removeClass('searchBoxEmpty');
        var emptyText = sbox.attr('data-empty');
        if ($.trim(sbox.val()).length == 0 || $.trim(sbox.val()) == emptyText) {
            sbox.addClass('searchBoxEmpty').val(emptyText).attr('placeholder', emptyText);
        }
    }

    var readCookie = function (name) {
        var regEx = new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;\\s*)" + name + "\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$", "");
        return document.cookie.replace(regEx, "$1");
    }
    var delete_cookie = function (name) {
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
        // document.cookie = name + '=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT; path=/';
        document.cookie = name + "=inactive; expires=" + d.toUTCString() + "; path=/";
    };
    $(function () {
        var jCookieName = "doNotDisplayJLinksCookie";

        var jCookieVal = readCookie(jCookieName);
        if (jCookieVal != "active") {
            $('.menu-cross').removeClass('cross-hidden');
            $('.jumplinks-menu-wrapper').removeClass('jlinks-menu-hidden');
        }

        $('.menu-button').on('click', function () {
            $('.menu-cross').toggleClass('cross-hidden');
            $('.jumplinks-menu-wrapper').toggleClass('jlinks-menu-hidden');
            if ($(".jumplinks-menu-wrapper").hasClass("jlinks-menu-hidden")) {
                var d = new Date();
                d.setTime(d.getTime() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
                document.cookie = jCookieName + "=active; expires=" + d.toUTCString() + "; path=/";
            }
            else {
                delete_cookie(jCookieName);
            }

        });
    });
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    function AddArrowsToUL(ul) {
        if (ul.data('side-arrow')) return;
        ul.data('side-arrow', 1);
        $('<div class="nav-side-arrow"><div class="right"></div></div>').insertBefore(ul).on('click', function () {
            var div = $(this).find('div');
            if (div.hasClass('right')) {
                div.removeClass('right').addClass('down');
                ul.slideDown('fast');
            }
            else {

                div.removeClass('down').addClass('right');
                div.parent().next().removeClass("menuShow").removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight");
                $(".mobile-mod-height").css("height", "inherit");
                ul.slideUp('fast');
            }
            return false;
        });
    }


    $(window).load(function () {


        /* When right pane empty and not in edit mode, make left pane full width */
        if ($('.RightPane h6').length == 0 && !$('body').is('.dnnEditState') && $('.RightPane .ModDNNHTMLC').length == 0) {

            $('.LeftPane').addClass("noRightPane");
        }

        /* Toggle User Properties Menu
        -------------------------------------------*/
        $('.userName a').click(function (e) {
            $(this).toggleClass('active');
            $('.userMenu').fadeToggle('fast');
            e.stopPropagation();
        });
        $(document.body).click(function () {
            $('.userMenu').hide();
            $('.userName a').removeClass("active");
        });
        $('#dnn_pnav li').mouseenter(function () {
            $('.userMenu').hide();
            $('.userName a').removeClass("active");
        });
        $('.userMenu').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });


        /* Set CSS3 Animations via class: http://daneden.me/animate/
        ---------------------------------------------*/
        $("#dnn_pnav li").hover(
             function () {
                 // detect viewport
                 var width = $(window).width();
                 if (width < 1400)
                     $("ul", this).removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight").addClass('fadeInDown rightDropdown');
                 else
                     $("ul", this).removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight").addClass('fadeInDown');
             },
             function () { $("ul", this).removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight").addClass('fadeOutUp'); }
         );
        $("#dnn_pnav li ul li").hover(
             function () { $("ul", this).removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight").addClass('fadeInLeft'); },
             function () { $("ul", this).removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight").addClass('fadeOutRight'); }
         );

        /* Mobile Menu
       ---------------------------------------------*/
        $('.mobileMenu > a').click(function () {
            if ($('ul#dnn_pnav').is(':visible')) {
                $('ul#dnn_pnav').slideUp('fast');
            }
            else {
                $('ul#dnn_pnav').slideDown('fast');
                $('ul#dnn_pnav > li > ul').each(function () {

							div.removeClass('down').addClass('right');
							div.parent().next().removeClass("menuShow").removeClass("fadeInDown fadeOutUp rightDropdown fadeInLeft fadeOutRight");
							$(".mobile-mod-height").css("height","inherit");
							ul.slideUp('fast');
						}
						return false;
					});
					*/

                $('ul#dnn_pnav > li > ul > li.secondary-arrow > ul').each(function () {

    var mouseLeaveFunc = function (className) {
        delayFunc($("." + className).children("ul"));
        $("." + className).removeClass(className);
    };

    var timeoutArray = [];

    var delayFunc = function ($obj) {
        $obj.removeClass("menuShow");
        //$obj.css("display", "none");
    };

    var addMenuShow = function ($obj) {
        $obj.addClass("menuShow");

        if ($(window).width() <= 1028) {
            var childlen = $obj.children().length;
            if (childlen > 0 && $obj.css('display') != "none") {
                var itemHeight = parseInt($obj.children().first().height().toString().replace("px", "")) + 5;
                if (itemHeight == 5) itemHeight = 38;
                var menuHeight = (itemHeight * childlen)
                if (menuHeight > 10) $obj.height(menuHeight);
                $obj.addClass("mobile-mod-height");
                if ($obj.parent().parent().hasClass("menuShow")) {
                    var $objparent = $obj.parent().parent();
                    childlen = $objparent.children().length;
                    itemHeight = parseInt($objparent.children().first().height().toString().replace("px", "")) + 5;
                    if (itemHeight == 5) itemHeight = 38;
                    menuHeight = menuHeight + (itemHeight * childlen);

                    if (menuHeight > 10) $objparent.height(menuHeight);
                    $objparent.addClass("mobile-mod-height");
                }
            }
        } else {
            $(".mobile-mod-height").css("height", "inherit");
        }
    };

    var mouseEnterFunc = function () {
        timeoutArray.forEach(function (aObj) {
            clearTimeout(aObj.id);
            delayFunc(aObj.selector);
        });
        timeoutArray = [];
    };

    $(function () {
        
        $('.skinWidth').each(function (i, obj) {
            var count = 0;
            $(obj).children("div").each(function (j) {

                if ($(this).attr("id")) {
                    if ($(this).attr("id").indexOf("dnn_GrayTop") > -1) {
                        count++;
                    }

                }
            });

            if (count == 3) {
                $(obj).css('width', '60%');
            }

            if (count == 2) {
                $(obj).css('width', '40%');

            }
        });


        $("#NavBar ul#dnn_pnav li").mouseenter(function () {
            mouseEnterFunc();
            addMenuShow($(this).children("ul"));
            mouseLeaveFunc('outertimeoutClass');
        });
        $("#NavBar ul#dnn_pnav li").mouseleave(function () {
            if ($(window).width() <= 1028) {
                $(this).addClass("outertimeoutClass");
            } else {
                $(this).addClass("outertimeoutClass");
                var id = setTimeout("mouseLeaveFunc('outertimeoutClass')", 200);
                var selector = $(this).children("ul");
                timeoutArray.push({ id: id, selector: selector });
            }
        });
        $("#NavBar ul#dnn_pnav > li > ul > li").mouseenter(function () {
            mouseEnterFunc();
            addMenuShow($(this).children("ul"));
        });
        $("#NavBar ul#dnn_pnav > li > ul > li").mouseleave(function () {
            $(this).addClass("innertimeoutClass");
            var id = setTimeout("mouseLeaveFunc('innertimeoutClass')", 200);
            var selector = $(this).children("ul");
            timeoutArray.push({ id: id, selector: selector });
        });
    });
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    //Custom Slider pagination functions
    function hideRemoveSmallDot(paginationClass) {
        brioSwiperHideRemoveSmallDot(paginationClass);
    }
    function brioSwiperHideRemoveSmallDot(paginationClass) {

        $(paginationClass + " span").css("display", "none");
        $(paginationClass + " span").removeClass("small-slider-dot");
    };

    function condShowAddSmallClass(paginationClass, index, modifier, bAddClass, bAddClassAnimate) {
        brioSwiperCondShowAddSmallClass(paginationClass, index, modifier, bAddClass, bAddClassAnimate);
    }
    function brioSwiperCondShowAddSmallClass(paginationClass, index, modifier, bAddClass, bAddClassAnimate) {

        if ($(paginationClass + " span").eq(index + modifier)) {
            $(paginationClass + " span").eq(index + modifier).show();
            if (bAddClass) {
                if (bAddClassAnimate) {
                    $(paginationClass + " span").eq(index + modifier).addClass("small-slider-dot", 400);
                }
                else {
                    $(paginationClass + " span").eq(index + modifier).addClass("small-slider-dot");
                }
            }
        }
    };

    function BrioSwiper(swiperContainerClass, swiperPaginationClass) {
        this.swiperContainerClass = swiperContainerClass;
        this.swiperPaginationClass = swiperPaginationClass;
        this.position = 0;
        this.direction = 0;
        var parent = this;
        var getSwiperObject = function (paginationClass) {
            var swiperobj = {
                pagination: {
                    el: parent.swiperPaginationClass,
                    dynamicBullets: true,
                    },
                paginationClickable: true,
            };

            return swiperobj;
        };
        var swiperobjz = getSwiperObject(swiperPaginationClass);

        //surethingggs
        this.swiper = new Swiper(swiperContainerClass, swiperobjz);
        return this.swiper;
    }
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    var scroll_pos = 0;
    var scroll_time;

    $(window).scroll(function () {
        if ($(window).width() > 1025) {
            clearTimeout(scroll_time);
            var current_scroll = $(window).scrollTop();

            if (current_scroll <= 1) {
                if (current_scroll <= scroll_pos) {
                    $('.topBar').fadeIn("slow", function () { $(this).removeClass('hidden'); });
                    $('.sticky-header').removeClass('sleek-header');
                    $('.sticky-breadcrumbs').removeClass('sleek-breadcrumbs');
                    $(".sleek-search").addClass("hidden");
                    $(".sleek-search span").addClass("hidden");
                    $(".search").removeClass("hidden").css("display", "inline-block");
                    $("#dnn_dnnSearch_ClassicSearch > a").css("display", "block");
                }
            }
            else {
                $('.topBar').fadeOut("slow", function () { $(this).addClass('hidden'); });
                $('.sticky-header').addClass('sleek-header');
                $('.sticky-breadcrumbs').addClass('sleek-breadcrumbs');
                $(".sleek-search").removeClass("hidden");
                $(".sleek-search i").removeClass("hidden");
                $(".search").removeClass("hidden").css("display", "none");

            }

            scroll_time = setTimeout(function () {
                scroll_pos = $(window).scrollTop();
            }, 50);
        }
    });
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {

        String.prototype.splice = function (idx, rem, str) {
            return this.slice(0, idx) + str + this.slice(idx + Math.abs(rem));
        };

        var _formContent = $(".tabbed-forms");

        var _requiredFieldClicked = false;

        var _selectedForms = {};

        if (_formContent) {

            $('.form-builder-canvas.Simple button').attr("style", "border-radius: 4px !important");

            $('.dnnPrimaryAction').each(function () {

                $(this).removeAttr('style');
                $(this).attr("style", "border-radius: 4px !important")
                $(this).addClass('dnn_form_submitbtn');
            })



            $('div.dnnLabel.required.form-canvas-label').each(function (i, obj) {


                var _reqField = "";

                if ($(obj).next().children().length > 1) {
                    $(obj).next().children().each(function () {
                        if ($(this).attr("class")) {
                            _reqField = $(this).attr("class");
                            return;
                        }
                    });
                }
                else if ($(this).next().attr("class")) {
                    _reqField = $(this).next().attr("class");
                }
                else if ($(this).next().find("input").attr("class")) {
                    _reqField = $(this).next().find("input").attr("class");
                }

                _reqField = _reqField.splice(0, 0, ".");

                _reqField = _reqField.replace(/ /g, ".");

                if (_reqField.slice(-1) == '.') {
                    _reqField = _reqField.replace(/.$/, "")
                }

                $(this).attr('id', 'formlabel_' + i);


                if (_reqField.length > 1) {


                    $(_reqField).click(function (j) {
                        if (!$(this).is("input")) {
                            $(this).css("color", "black");
                            $(this).parent().prev().css("color", "black");
                            _selectedForms[$(this).parent().prev().attr('id')] = $(this);
                        }
                    });

                    //$(_reqField).change(function () {

                    //    if ($(_reqField).next()) {
                    //        if (!$(_reqField).next('div').attr("class")) {
                    //                $(this).css("color", "black");
                    //                $(this).parent().prev().css("color", "black");
                    //                _selectedForms[$(this).parent().prev().attr('id')] = $(this);
                    //                $(this).prev().css("color", "black");
                    //        }
                    //    }

                    //});

                    $(_reqField).keyup(function () {

                        if ($(_reqField).val().length > 0) {
                            $(this).css("color", "black");
                            $(this).parent().prev().css("color", "black");

                            $(this).prev().css("color", "black");

                            var _id = "";
                            if ($(this).parent().prev().attr('id')) {
                                _id = $(this).parent().prev().attr('id');
                            }
                            else {
                                _id = $(this).prev().attr('id');
                            }

                            _selectedForms[_id] = $(this);



                        }
                    });

                }
            })


            $(".dnnPrimaryAction").click(function () {
                if ($(this).text().toLowerCase() == "submit") {

                    setTimeout(function () {
                        var _errorListChildren = $('.error-message');
                        var _firstItem = false;
                        $('div.dnnLabel.required.form-canvas-label').each(function (i) {
                            if (!_selectedForms[$(this).attr('id')]) {
                                $(this).css("color", " #e1529d");

                                if (!_firstItem) {

                                    $('html, body').animate({
                                        scrollTop: $(this).offset().top - 215
                                    }, 1000, 'swing', function () { });
                                }

                                _firstItem = true;
                            }
                        })

                    }, 50);

                }
            });
        }
    })
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {

        function CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn(obj) {
            $(obj).children('a').each(function () {
                if ($(obj).text().indexOf("*~") > -1 && $(obj).text().indexOf("~*") > -1) {
                    $(this).addClass("dark-button")

                }
            });


            //$(obj).children('a').each(function () {
            //    if ($(obj).text().indexOf("*~") > -1) {
            //        $(obj)[0].innerHTML = $(obj)[0].innerHTML.replace("~*", "");
            //        $(obj)[0].innerHTML = $(obj)[0].innerHTML.replace("*~", "");
            //    }
            //});
            for (var i = 0; i < obj.length; i++) {
                $(obj)[i].innerHTML = $(obj)[i].innerHTML.replace(/[~*]/g, '');;
                $(obj)[i].innerHTML = $(obj)[i].innerHTML.replace(/[*~]/g, '');;


            }


        }

        var _divElement = $("div:contains(~*)");
        var _pElement = $("p:contains(~*)");
        var _spanElement = $("span:contains(~*)");
        var _liElement = $("li:contains(~*)");
        var hTagList = [];

        for (var i = 1; i < 7; i++) {
            if ($("h" + i + ":contains(~*)").length > 0) {
                CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn($("h" + i + ":contains(~*)"))
            }
        }

        if (_pElement.length > 0) {

            CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn(_pElement);
        }
        if (_spanElement.length > 0) {

            CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn(_spanElement);
        }
        if (_liElement.length > 0) {

            CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn(_liElement);
        }
        if (_divElement.length > 0) {
            CheckAndSetIfElementIsBtn(_divElement);
        }

    });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {

        // Find all elements that are links in the body tag
        var aTags = $('body').find('a[href*="http"]');

        
        // loop through each and every links 
        for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
            if ($(aTags[i]).attr('href')) {
                // check if each tag has a full domain on it i.e. http://www 
                // if the a link has a full domain, open the add target = blank attribute to the current element.
                if ($(aTags[i]).attr('href').indexOf('www.siam.org') < 0 &&  $(aTags[i]).attr('href').indexOf('evoq-eval.siam.org') < 0) {
                    $(aTags[i]).prop('target', '_blank');
                }
            }

        }

    });
   </script>
   <script>
    $(document).ready(function() {

    $("a[href*='mailto:']").each(function(){
        if($(this).attr('href').indexOf('@') == -1 && $(this).attr('href').indexOf('.') == -1)
        {
            var newUrl = $(this).attr('href').replace('mailto:', '/Forms/Contact-SIAM?popUp=true&e=');
            $(this).attr('data-src', newUrl);
            $(this).attr('data-fancybox','');
            $(this).attr('data-type',"iframe");
            $(this).attr('href', "javascript:;");
        }
    });
                  
});
   </script>
